Though you may be providing valid headers and keys you might\nstill receive a 401 Unauthorized response based on the permissions of the key.\n\nThe Data API uses standard HTTP request methods DELETE, GET (read), POST (create) and\nPATCH (update). Below is the list of their respective successful response codes:\n\n    GET    200\n    POST   201\n    PATCH  200\n    DELETE 204\n\nAdditional documentation can be found at \u003Chttps://docs.gibsonai.com/#api-usage\u003E",
